            // Use the window load event to keep the page load performant
            window.addEventListener('load', function() {
                navigator.serviceWorker.register("/store/epic-service-worker.js", {scope: '/store/'})

    }
})();

   (function () {
    if (window.SharedWorker) {
        try {
            var statsWorker = new SharedWorker('/store/epic-analytics-worker.js', 'epic-analytics-worker');
            statsWorker.port.start();
            window.__statsWorker = statsWorker;
        } catch (e) {
            console.error("Error starting analytics worker");
        }
    } else if (window.Worker) {
        try {
            window.__statsWorker = new Worker('/store/epic-analytics-worker.js');
        } catch (e) {
            console.error("Error starting analytics worker");
        }
    } else {
        console.error("Workers not supported in this browser");
    }
})();
